<font color="#000000" size="3" face="Times New Roman">

</font><p style="margin: 0cm 0cm 10pt;" class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-NZ"><font color="#000000" size="3" face="Calibri">There are some similar rows that can
probably be considered as groups.</font></span></p><font color="#000000" size="3" face="Times New Roman">

</font><p style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt 36pt; text-indent: -18pt; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo3;" class="MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst"><font color="#000000"><span style="font-family: Symbol; mso-fareast-font-family: Symbol; mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol;" lang="EN-NZ"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;"><font size="3">·</font><span style='font: 7pt/normal "Times New Roman"; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal;'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><span lang="EN-NZ"><font size="3" face="Calibri">Dependants, History, Logs and
Preview screens are effectively read-only screens and consequently, the user
always has access to these screens regardless of asset status.</font></span></font></p><font color="#000000" size="3" face="Times New Roman">

</font><p style="margin: 0cm 0cm 10pt 36pt; text-indent: -18pt; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo3;" class="MsoListParagraphCxSpLast"><font color="#000000"><span style="font-family: Symbol; mso-fareast-font-family: Symbol; mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol;" lang="EN-NZ"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;"><font size="3">·</font><span style='font: 7pt/normal "Times New Roman"; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal;'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><span lang="EN-NZ"><font size="3" face="Calibri">Permissions, Metadata Schemas,
Layouts and Workflow (With the exception of approving or rejecting, as noted
below) screens require admin access to make changes, so the user with write
permission only, never has access.</font></span></font></p><font color="#000000" size="3" face="Times New Roman">

</font><p style="margin: 0cm 0cm 10pt;" class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-NZ"><font color="#000000" size="3" face="Calibri">The following table indicates which screens
on the admin interface a user with write permission to assets with workflow
applied that is not the approval step in workflow.</font></span></p><font color="#000000" size="3" face="Times New Roman">
